The paper proposes using cross-post networks to analyze Usenet newsgroups' community structure, revealing small-world properties and presenting a spectral clustering algorithm for topical classification, with contributions from authors like Kensuke Onuma, Belle L. Tseng, Amin Saberi, and others.
The paper discusses efficient feature selection methods for high-dimensional scientific datasets, with contributions from authors Chandrika Kamath, Shawn Newsam, and Erick Cantu-Paz, covering challenges and strategies in astronomy, plasma physics, and remote sensing.
The paper proposes a general ensemble method incorporating data quality matrices to enhance predictive accuracy by reducing variance, with contributions from authors Ian Davidson, Giri K. Tayi, Ashish Grover, and Ashwin Satyanarayana.
The paper presents an automated two-step system for mapping supplier part numbers in BOMs to internal part numbers, involving authors Jayant Kalagnanam, Yuk Wah Wong, Moninder Singh, Michael Patek, and Sudhir Verma, to replace manual processes and improve efficiency.
The paper proposes a real-time topic trend analysis framework using a dynamically learned finite mixture model, with insights from experts like Daniel Huttenlocher, Andrew McCallum, and Christos Faloutsos.
The paper proposes a travel time prediction method using probe-car data with AR models and state space models, co-authored by Jun-ichi Takeuchi and Takayuki Nakata, demonstrating effectiveness in Nagoya.
The paper demonstrates SQL's efficient implementation of K-means clustering with linear scalability, supported by authors specializing in data mining, database optimization, and machine learning.
The paper explores heuristic document preprocessing techniques (IDF, normalization, log transformations) to enhance naive Bayes and multinomial mixture clustering, with contributions from authors like Shyam Kapur, Wen-tau Yih, and others.
The paper explores machine learning methods for metabolomic data classification, with contributions from authors Xiaodong Lin, Young Truong, and Chris Beecher, addressing challenges in disease biochemistry analysis.
The paper introduces Analytical View (AV) in MBF for OLTP-OLAP integration, with contributions from authors Jonathan Tang, Sam Skrivan, Adam Yeh, and Youxuan Jin.
